BUZANI KUMKABAYI
 
ISAHLUKO I 
AMAWELE 
Kwakusebusika ngoNtulikazi, izulu lihoshe ishisandlu. Hanga lase liphurnile kuyikhona irnisebe yalo isathi ieashacosha isithwathwa esabe sirnhlophe wu eziqongweni zeSihlungu neNhlazalshe kanye nezinye izintaba eziphakerne. Phansi kwaNobarnba kwakuthule kuthe du, kwazise phela iNdlunkulu yenkosi uJarna kwakulalwe ibika irnisiko. Yikho lokhu okwenza ukuba uJarna asheshe avuke. Kuthe esabhunga nenceku yakhe uManqina, kwezwakala isigijirni sesimhasha: 
UJaMa kaNdaba, 
UJaMa kalulhwana kangakanani, Nasenhlamvini yomkhont' angenela, Nasengatsheni angaphathelela. 
1 

 
 
Obengumgingo wanga itshe laseZihlalo, Ebelingalayezwa ngabaphath' izinhlendla, Thina bamaklwa singathath' ichoba sophule. UMabopha wakithi kwaZwangendaba, Ongibophe zaluk' inhlazane nemfuduluko. Obabis' ihlaba elikuMahogo, 
Othabis' idukumbane elikuNgcingci. Owahlafun' umlom' engadli lutho ... 
Asibange sisaghubeka isigijimi lokhu uJama owabe omele umbiko ophathelene neNdlunkulu yakhe wamkhakhabisa kabi uMangina, ethi akangenise lowo okhulekayo. Nebala uMangina wenza njengoba ethunyiwe, wangena naso isigijimi, bakhuleka bobabili: "'Wen a weNdlovu! Bayede!" 
"Ungabe usakhuleka, mfokazana ndini! Ndaba zini oza nazo?" 
Kubuza uJama amehlo eseggamuka in hI ansi yomlilo, izwi lihlaba njengosungulo. Akazenzi belu uJama, ubuthongo wayengazange abuthi guthu ngalobobusuku ngenxa yokuzibika kwenkosikazi yakhe. Phela iNdlunkulu lena yayinzima, futhi sekuyizinsuku zokuba ikhululeke. Ngaphandle nje kokuthi yayingumuntu obuthaka, yayibuye futhi ihlushwe yimbeleko. Sikhuluma nje uJama wayengakabi namntwana yize wayesemnkatsha ubomvu. Wayekhathazekileke ngombuso wakwaZulu, enexhala lokuthi nxa engahle abizwe ngoyisemkhulu engayishiyile induku ebandla, ubukhosi buyothathwa yindlu yasekhohlo, kokunye kudaleke imibango. Wacabanga ngemizamo kayise uNdaba, yokwakha uZulu abe yisizwe esiginile, ayeke ukugonelwa yimibuso yawoButhelezi neyawoLanga wakwaNdwandwe. Wabona ukuthi imizamo kayise izophihlizeka phansi kwezakhe izandla nxa kughubeka kanje. 
  Akuyikho njalo ukuthi wayengabatholi abantwana. Empeleni iNdlunkulu yayifike yazibula ngomfana uPhalo kodwa akaphilanga, washeshe wabizwa ngoyisemkhulu. Kanti nakho ukushona kwakhe kwamane kwaba yindida nje, ukuba umntwana aphogoke okwezele lommbila, kungasenziwanga nazaba. Kuthe kusuka lapho kwase kwala imbeleko, in kosi yaze yasizwa yinyanga yasezansi ngasoNgoye eyafike yenza izihlambezo ezashaya emhlolweni, yakhulelwa iNdlunkulu. Nanxa ukukhulelwa kwayo kwaletha intokozo enkulu kwaNobamba, lokhu kwaphelezelwa wukuxhwala kwayo ... 
  "Ngibuza kuwe, mfokazana ndini, ngithi injani iNdlunkulu?" kufutheka uJama esalokhu ebajamele. 
2 
  "Ndlov' enamandla! Ndlovu edla nabasondezeli bayo! Wen a kaPhunga noMageba! INdlunkulu iyaphila, Silo samakhosi!" kuphendula isigijimi ngelivevezelayo. 
  Kwathi xhifi kuJama esecabanga ngokuthi ukuba kakwengabi isiko, ngabe uziyela yen a lapho iNkosikazi ikhona, ayozibonela, kunokuzama ukughwanda umbiko kulesisigijimi esesikhungatheke ngaloluhlobo. Yinto azoyithini nje kodwa lena? Nokho aphonse omunye futhi umbuzo: "Manje usho ukuthi okuzele lapha wuktlZongitshela ukuthi iNdlunkulu iyaphila nje gha?" 
"Qha, Mageba, kakunjalo. Ngizobika wena weZulu eliphezulu! 
Ngizobika ukuthi iNdlunkulu isikhululekile, Ndabezitha! Futhi iphumelele kahle wena weNdlovu!" 
  "Pho nxa iNdlunkulu iphumelele kahle yini eyenza ukuba umiwe yisidwa? Awungitsheli ngani ukuthi ithole mntwana muni? Uyashinga, mfokazana ndini?" kusho inkosi isukuma esigqikini saya, okwenza noMangina athi ukwethuka, esebona ukuthi udaba seluze lwega amadolo. 
  "Yethula umbiko oze ngawo, wethu, uphelele. Wenzani Mswelazonke ukuba ucogise in kosi uyindoda ngikwethembile na?" kusho yena uMangina ebhekise kuMswelazonke, isigijimi, nakhu esebona ukuthi ithunga lizogcwala amanzi. Kumcacele noMswelazonke ukuthi sekukubi. Athi esaninga itulo, imkhakhabise futhi inkosi. 
"Ngitshele libelinye mfokazana, ngumfana noma yintombazana?" "Ndabezitha! Kakusiyena umfana." 
"Pho nxa kungeyena umfana wehlulwa yini ukuthi yintombazana? 
Wehlulwa yini ukuphendula umbuzo wami, Mswelazonke?" 
  "Umbuzo wakho unzima, Mageba! Nami ngilahlwe ngabaphansi ukuba kube yimina engijutshelwe ukuletha lombiko ezindlebeni zenkosi. Mageba, kakumfana, kakuntombazana, kepha ngama ... ngama ... ngama ... ngamantombazana ... e ... e ... " Waphelelwa ngamazwi uMswelazonke. 
UJama waphendula amehlo wabheka emseleni, watshaka amathe. 
Wabuyela esiggikini sakhe wahlala wathi khehlehle. Washo ngeliphansi wathi: "Wo! Bala! Ngiyezwa, mfokazana ndini ... Usho ukuthi abaphansi bangi ... bangi ... bangi ... " 
. Wayefuna ukuthi; "Abaphansi bangishwabulele ngamawele." 
Nokho ayemesinda lawomazwi. Abaphansi kabajeziswa. Pho angabahlambalaza kanjani athi bamgalekisile na? Kungembangele imiswazi emibi kwakhona lokho? Kodwa iqiniso elimsulwa kwakuyilo lona lelo lokuthi umuzi wakwaNobamba wabe uhaqwe ngamashwa 
3 




 
namashwangusha. Elinye lalawomashwa kwakuwukuba iNkosikazi yaseNdlunkulu izale amawele kanti bekulindelwe inkosana. Nokwenza amawele lawo ngamantombazana ... 
  Yaphenduka in kosi yabheka ngasemsamo manje, endaweni yamathongo, kwaze kwaba sengathi ifuna ukuthetha idlozi, ibuze ukuthi kanti yoneni. Yayihlale izwa kuthiwa abaphansi yizithutha, kodwa ibingalindele ukuthi sebeyizithutha kangako, ukuba sebengaze bavumele okunje kwehlele umuzi wabo. Bathi bayokhonzwa ngubani nxa lomuzi wakwaNobamba bewuyeka ushabalala? Nokho lemidlinzo yayo kayizange iyiphimisele. Kwakwesinda ngisho ukuba ivule umlomo. Ngomzuzwana, ibunzi laya labe seligeleza izithukuthuku, ezinhlafunweni kwase kuqanse imilhambo, isilokhu iququda imihlathi, kanti amehlo wona selokhu egqolozele ndawonye khona lapho emsamo. Kwakubona ngisho ekhasela eziko ukuthi, qhabo bo, lomuntu ujulile ngemicabango. 
  Makhathaleni ithombuluke inkosi: "Sengiwuzwile umbiko wakho, Mswelazonke. Ubatshele eNdlunkulu ukuthi ngizwile. Okwamanje seningaphuma kanye nawe Manqina, keningishiye ngedwa ngininge ngaloludabakazi." 
  Nebala bakhuleka oManqina noMswelazonke qede baphuma, beshiya inkosi yamaZulu ihlalisene nemicabango. 
4 
ISAHLUKO 2 
UKUGINGISA IGABADE 
Bedlula ubusika kwangena intwasahlobo. lzulu lakhuphula izitsha, lehlisa amaconsi emvula, izwe lonke labancwaba, izihlahla namagquma sekwembethe ingubo eluhlaza. Kwasekuzwakala njalo ngokuhlwa amaxoxo exokozela, ehaya inkondlo yawo yokubonga inala yamanzi. 
  Safika isikhathi sokuba uJama kaNdaba afeze isiko, abize abantwana azobabona, abethe amagama abo qede abakhunge. Kuthe angalunquma usuku lokulethwa kwabo elawini lakhe, amakhosikazi ozalo awa ngamadolo sekuphiswa utshwala bomkhosi lowo omkhulukazi. 
  Lwafika olungaliyo lwejadu, uZulu waphelela ngezinkani kwaNobamba. Laphaya esigodlweni sekulungiswa abantwana begezwa, begcotshwa nangensindane. Kwaba yilowo wagqiza ngobuhlalu 
5 




 
obumhlophe ezihlakaleni, wabe esebhinea ueu lwamaqanda amhlophe okhalo. Unina naye wadiliza imvunulo yakhe kanokusho, esethunge inhloko yakhe entsha lokhu phela kade ephucile, nasemzimbeni kade eluhlaza, engavunule. Lolu kwakulusuku olukhulu kuye - usuku lokuphuma exhibeni, abuyele elawini lakhe; abone noyise wabantwana ayelokhu amgcina engakangeni kulelixhiba ukuzobeletha. 
  Nokho injabulo yakhe yayingaphelele. Kwakungafani naleliyalanga mhla ezokwethula uPhalo phambi kwenkosi. Phela ngalelolanga wayegqishazela. Egqishazela kumfanele lokhu inkosi yakhe nesizwe sonke sakwaZulu wayeyizalele indlalifa nenkosana. Kanti akabuzanga elangeni, abaphansi bazosheshe bamthathe uPhalo, kuyathi eselanywa, uselanywa ngamawele ... 
  Kwathi lapho ekueabanga konke lokhu wafikelwa zinyembezi ezagala zingamaconsi zathi zisuka zaziwohloka zithi rni ... zigeleza ngezihlathi kuhle kwemvula yomvimbi. lzintombi zasesigodlweni zazama ukumduduza, zimtshela ukuthi kungebe kuhle ukuba afike phambi kwenkosi enamehlo abomvu akhombisa ukuthi kade ekhihla isililo. Nebala wazama ukuzibamba kepha salokhu sibelesele isilokozane sokuthi kazi woneni kangaka kwabaphansi bangaze bamfulathele na. 
  Kwase kuyisikhathi sakhe sokuba aphume lesi kepha wathi uyema wafikelwa yisiyezi. Ekhanda kwakhala izihlonono. Umuzi wakwaNobamba waba yidwala elihlezi emahlombe akhe, wamesinda. Nempela wawusunesinye isithunzi manje. Ingani laphaya esibayeni uZulu wayesengangoboya bendlovu - kuphelele izikhulu zezwe, oNkwelo noMhlaba, abafowabo benkosi. OMudli babekhona lapho, kukhona futhi abakwaMpungose, izinsika zombuso kaZulu; bekhona futhi noSibiya, nabanye. Nabo njalo beyisikhomololo bekhulumela phansi, bengunaza ezisematheni zokuzalwa kwamawele eNdlunkulu ... 
  Nokho igeine izijubiJe iNdlunkulu, ithathe iphangela elikhihliza ingwebu emhlophe ilithi ze ekhanda, iqonde elawini lenkosi. Abazanyana balandele betete abantwana. Abasebahle lapho abantwana ungathi bayakhangisa. Sebede bemamatheka ngeziklumana zezihlathi, baveze izifaea, bengazi nokuthi lidumephi. 
  Ikhuleke iNdlunkulu, ayingenise uManqina, ineeku enkulu ehlezi nenkosi uJama kanye namaphakathi akwaNobamba, imihlalandlini phela. Ingene qede ibeke phansi iphangela layo iNdlunkulu. Intombazana iyinike isikhetho nembala ikhethe ngesinono ithi ingaqeda 
6 
ithathe inkezo ikhe ephangeleni isiphungula phela. I1wesule kahle ukhamba bese iJubeka phambi kwenkosi uJama, ibisikhuleka. Nanso isisuka isiyohlala esininini sawomame, iqhetha lapho nabazanyana abaphethe abantwana laba abazobona uyise. 
  UJama yena uhlezi esigqikini. AkayibhekiJe inkosikazi ezinhlamvini zamehlo, kepha ude eyeba esiqwini sornzimba, amehlo wona anamathele kubantwana. Ubagqolozele sengathi ufuna ukubona ngaphakathi ezibiJini zabo. Emva kwesikhathi awabuyise amehlo, abheke okhambeni. Athathe inkezo ngesinono avonxe okhambeni, aphuze. Ehlise amathanyana ambalwa bese eqikiJeka ehlina lokhu phela bamphisele inhlaba. Abuye ampempeshele, ayiminye inkezo. Ajube ukuba uManqina aphuze futhi aphuzise nebandla lonke. Abhekise kuNdlunkulu enxusa ukuba kulethwe abantwana ababone. 
Ithi ukukhophozela iNdlunkulu bese ikhuleka ithi: "Bayede, wena 
waphakathi!" Ithathe umntwana kumzanyana ifike iguqe naye phambi kwenkosi. Inkosi imemukele, imbheke. Umntwana eqala ukuzwa izandla zikayise naye abhekise amehlo akhe kuleliphevu, babhekane. UJama nendodakazi bajamelane. Muhle umntwana lona, ubuso yisimomondiya, amehlo aqhakaziJe kuhle kwezinkanyezi kepha akhanya inhlansi yomlilo. Imbheke ingane uyise ingathi ewayi, kuze kuewayize yena. Emveni kokuthula isikhathi eside, ezwakale uJama ethi ukuthinta isikhwehlela qede athi: "Igama lalomntwana nguMkabayi." 
. INdlunkulu kanye namaphakathi onke bakhuleke bathi: "Bayede, wena omnyama!" benanela ukwethiwa komntwana. lsukume iN dlunkulu iye enkosini, yelule izandla isiJungisela ukumthatha umntwana lokhu useliqanjiwe igama; kepha uJama amgomoshele umntwana, kube sengathi ulaIele imfudumalo yakhe. Kubenzima ukwehlukana naye. Amehlo omntwana ayizimbulunga asuke abuyise engqondweni kaJama umfanekiso kayise uNdaba, yena owayenamehlo akhanya inhlansi yomliJo. Nangaso lesisikhathi ingane isalokhu imgqolozele uyise, imbuka khona kanye ezinhlamvini zamehlo. Amehlo kaMkabayi ayexoxa indaba, uJama wakuphawula lokho, kuphela wayeswele ozomehazela noma amhumushele leyondaba. Warnwota umntwana emsondeza kuye, wezwa ukufudumala kwegazi lakhe Iiveneneza ngemithambo yonke yomzimba, lifuthwa yisigaxana senhliziywana. Walizwa nelakhe igazi lifudumala uJama. Inhliziyo yakhe yaduduza ngamandla, izingalo zangenwa yidumbe, zaqhaqhazela. Igazi elaligijima emithanjeni kaMkabayi kwakuligazi 
7 




 
lakhe uJama. Lela kwakuliginiso elingeguguke, yize uMkabayi eliwele ... 
  "Usungamthatha uMkabayi, Nkosikazi, ungilethele omunye naye ngimethe," sekusho uJama emanga esiphongweni, ezihlathini kanye nasemlonyeni. Benanele elawini ngokukhuleka: "Bayede! Wena waphakathi!" 
  Nokho bonke baphawule ukuthi izwi likaJama liyagedezela. Isukume ngentobeko iNdlunkulu imthathe uMkabayi imnike umzanyana. Iphendukele kulomzanyana ohleli ngezansi bese ithatha owesibili umntwana imuse kuyise. Amemukele uJama. Ambheke. Kepha lomntwana abe namahloni, akhophokhophoze njengonina, amehlo ehluleke ukuhlangana nakayise. Izindebe zomntwana zithuthumele, zila zehlukana zihlangana. Nazo futhi zazifuze ezikanina. Empeleni kuningi okukulomntwana athi lapho embheka uJama amfumanise efuze unina, iNdlunkulu yakwaNobamba, intandokazi yakhe. Nebala-ke amethe umntwana athi nguMmama, kudume uBayede endlini sekwenanela amaphakathi. 
  Amgone emsondeza kuye kepha uMmama azexwaye izandla zendoda, adazuluke akhale. Abasendlini bag ale bawesasele lomsindo wokukhala ngoba ukuthula obesekukhona besebehluleka ukukubekezelela. Bekufana nokuthula okwelanywa nguzamcolo nesai1ggurna. Kepha kuthe lapho umntwana eghubeka nokukhala, izwi lakhe lahlaba njengosungulo, wakhala njengomuntu omdala ekhihla isililo kufiwe. Izwi lakhe labanga umunyu, ekhala ngosizi nokuzincengela sengathi uyazi ukuthi uliwele ... 
  UJama ezwe sekushisa izinkophe. Bobabili abantwana benza ukuba akhale izinyembezi ezehla ngesifuba. Anxuse ukuba iNdlunkulu isale isimthatha uMmama. Nakunina aghubeke nokukhala uMmama, kwehlule noma esexhunywe ebeleni. 
  UJama aphelelwe ngamandla nesibindi send ada, aphenduke inina. Abheke iphangela eliphambi kwakhe, abone ukuthi yilo kuphela elingammisa idolo. Athathe inkezo aphuze. Leyo ayigojele engazange ayiphumule1e. Avonxe futhi okwesibili, athele umuthi enkomeni, aphinde futhi okwesithathu ampempeshele. Nebala asithole isibindi sokubikela indlu ukuthi akuphunywe kuyiwe esibayeni ukuze akhombise abantwana impahla abakhunga ngayo. Nempela bakhukhule sebegonde khona esibayeni. 
  Lithe ukuba libabone ibandla, lasukuma lonke ngothi Iwalo. Izwakale imbongi isibongela. Kumthinte kakhulu uJama ukuthi imbongi lena igale ngezibongo zikayise uNdaba. Phela sekungokwesibili

kusile ukuba akhunjuzwe ngoNdaba. Ingathi phela namehlo kaMkabay' amkhumubuze yena uNdaba! Nokho wayengenakuyithulisa ~mbongl yenza umsebenzi wayo. Hhayi-ke! Ighubeke imbongi lbonge:

  INdlunkulu yayingaphandle kwesibaya kunye nabazanyana ababephethe abantwana. Abafana bangenisa izinkomo, uJama wayesebakhunga abantwana. Wagala ngoMkabayi, wamkhunga ngogebedu lwenkone, :vayeseza kuMmama wamkhunga ngesiqengqe esimaganda kaway,ba. Wayesejuba ukuba kubulawe ezinye izinkabi 
9 




 
ezine ukuze abantu badle benele, wajuba futhi ukuba umhlabi nomhlinzi wezinkomo enze umsebenzi wakhe. Uthe esuka wabe esecela ukuba umntwana uNkwelo abe yiso lakhe, yena wabe esebuyela endlini. 
Linkonone kakhulu ibandla, ikakhulukazi izikhulu zombuso. 
Zona zibona ukuthi inkosi ibhimbile ukuba iwakhunge omabili amawele. Lokho kwakuzobathukuthelisa abaphansi, kulethe nemiswazi emibi, inkosi noma iNdlunkulu behlelwe ngamashwa. lbandla ligdne ngokujuba abantwana oNkwelo noMhlaba ukuba bayobonisana nenkosi ngalomhlolo ewugilayo. Nempela bahambe oNkwelo kepha bemadolonzima, besindwa wudaba abazolubhunga nenkosi. Besindwa nayikho nje ukubhekana nenkosi kwazise yayingasandbilikile kahle selokhu kwazalwa amaphahla lana. Yayingasayi ngisho ukuyokotha ibandla. Ngabe bazoyingena ingeneke kodwa? Pho babezothini lokhu base bedliwe yinkatho. Banikele elawini lenkosi, bakhuleke maqede uManqina abangenise. 
  "Hhawu! Bantwana! Kanli yini enikhulekayo? Nangilandela ezithendeni nje, sekuphelile njalo ukuhlinza?" kubuza uJama ekhombisa ukungabenameli abafowabo. 
  "Wena waphakathi! Kunjalo, Luhlanga Iwezwe! Sekllphelile ukuhlinza," kuphendula uNkwelo ngenkathi akha izithanga esikhunjeni, ngezansi kwenceku yakoMkhulu, uManqina. 
  "Pho, tshelani amabutho ose izoso, kuthi eyezipheko in gene ezimbizeni. Ningakwenza kanjani ukuba nibuye nizonambithisisa kimi izinto kanti bese ngithena ningamehlo ami na? Yenzani konke, Mntwana, niphethe, mina ngizwa umzimba wami ngingawuzwa kahle, ngifisa ukuba kengithi llkucambalala." 
/lNdaba, kasizile kuwe ukuzonambithisisa ngezoso nezipheko. 
Lokho kuzophethwa njengesiko ... " 
  "Wo! Bala-ke khona! Kanti umthetho wenu nize ngani pho?" kubllza uJama, enquma uNkwelo ulimi. 
  "Sithunywe yisizwe, Mageba. Uma in kosi idunguzela, klldunguzela izwe lonke. Ngokunjalo-ke, Malandela, njengoba Udllbuzeke umzimba nje, nathi sonke imizimba idubuzekile. Siyesaba, Mageba, sesaba imiswazi nemikhokha ernzini wenkosi. Isizwe besethembilc, Mageba, ukuthi inkosi izokwenza isiko lesizwe elaziwayo. Ukungagcinwa kwesiko kwenza isizwe sesabe sithuthumele. Sesabela impi10 yakho Ndaba, sesabela ikusasa likaZulu. Siyesaba, wen' omnyarna!" Agwinye amathe uNkwelo, esanika inkosi ithuba lokuba ikiphefumllle.

Kwethwasa intwasahlobo yesihlanu bazalwa oMkabayi noMmama. Babezikhulela nje njengabantwana bonke. Isimanga wukuthi babethokozelwa ngabazali babo kuphela. Kwakuhlupheka yen a uMmama lowo owayekhonze ukudlala. Wayekhala ekhalile, izingane zimkhipha inyumbazana. Ayemakhulu eyizimbulunga kodwa emahle emhlophe. Abantu baqala ngokumenyanya kodwa ekukhuleni kwakhe bageina sebemesaba. Abaningi babeqinisa ukuthi mukhulu umuga oyogeina wenziwe yileliwele okwakumele ligingiswe igabade.

hleki naye. Okwakumcasula du wukuthi uMmama wayeyisitetemi. Wakhula uMkabayi, kwalindwa kwaZulu.

  Langena ihlobo, kwaqhilika inala ezweni. NeNdlunkulu yewukela esifeni sayo esiphezu koMhlathuze yafike yafula yagcwalisa iqoma. Yayizizwa ingconywana kulezizinsuku. Nokho uMkabayi owayesaba yinsila yayo wayekhona ehambisana nayo, esho nokuyithwalela iqoma kepha yona yale ithi usemncane.

Amantombazana asesigodlweni athatha ngokuthi icotshwe yilanga lokhu lalibalele likhipha umkhovu etsheni. Ayisiza-ke eyilalisa ukuba iphumule. Nebala ayishiya isizicambalalele phansi iNdlunkulu, aqhubeka nemisebenzi yawo yemihla ngemihla. 
  Empeleni lalibalele licoba ilanga. Kwakungabuzwa ukuthi Iingahle line. Kusenjalo liqale ukuhloma. Libuyise amafu amnyama. Ngokuphazima kweso kundize amahlolamvula. Ph ansi laphaya emfundeni yoMhlathuze sekude kubabaza izinsingizi ezimbili. Kusenjalo Iiphose izinkwimbi zemibani kukhontshobale izinja ziyozifihla phansi kwezinqolobane. Lidume lindindizele liphinde lidume liqaqambe. Kube kubi impela, izinyanga zikhiphe abafana bezulu sekuxega amabheshu. Lithele isihlambi sibe sinye bese kulandela isibhicongo sesangquma. Singashayi isangquma siphihlize, sivithize wen a mmbila, kubhubhe wena mbuzi wen a nkomo. Imifula igcwale 
20 
idle izindwani ngomzuzu, imvula ibe ngamathantala. Bonke abantu sebetshobele ezindlini, phandle akusakhashi lutho. 
  Makhathaleni Iinqamuke izulu. Abantu bathole isithuba sokuphefumula. Kube yikhona bephuma behlola nomonakalo owenziwe yizulu. Kulaba abayaluzayo kayikho iNdlunkulu. Akekho futhi noMkabayi. Kube yima kukhunjulwa ukuthi konje iNdlunkulu ibibike umzimba obuthaka. Izintombi zesigodlo zinikele khona eNdlunkulu. Nxa zingena emnyango zethuke zishoqongane nxa zalamela iNdlunkulu igobodise phezu kweziko. UMkabayi olokhu ehlezi ngezansi kukanina azibheke ngokumangala. Zibuze ukuthi iNdlunkulu isinjani angaziphenduli, adimede aziqhunsulele amehlo nje, nazo zimeqe ngaphezulu ziyokuzwa ukuthi ngabe iNdlunkulu igobodise . nje izizwa isinjani. Zithe nxa zithi ziyayiphendula, zafica ukuthi isiyabanda. Zethuke nazo kubande kwamancane. Zithi zibheka amehlo, zihlangane namhlophe, inhlamvu emnyama ayisabonwa. Zehluleke ukuzibamba, kusuke esinamathambo isidumo sezithwele imikhono ekhanda zidinda isililo. Zinikele kuManqina, inceku yakoMkhulu. Zithi zingambikela naye asukumele phezulu ezozibonela. Afike adelele khona ukuthi iNdlunkulu isithule. Kube yisimanga ukufa komuntu engagulanga. Kucace futhi ukuthi akuwona umphezulu lona kepha iNdlunkulu ithathwe ngukufa. Konje kuzothiwa kufa kuni? Kuzobuzwa kubani lokhu yon a isithule? Siqhubeke isililo. UMmama asizwe isililo ekwenye indlu, aye eNdlunkulu esentantatheka umntwana. Kazi khona okumsuse kude kangaka azokweshela lapha emajukujukwini yini? Wazibona ebamkhulu ebaluleka emhlabeni wonke uMkabayi. Kanti uhleli nje usaziwa ngisho kude Ie koNtunjambili? Phela yen a ubengazi ukuthi lendawo yakwaNtunjambili ikhona ngernpela. Ubethatha ngokuthi nje lelo yizwe lasezinganekwaneni; izwe lawoDemane noDemazane ahahlabelela bathi: "Litshe likaNtunjambili, litshe likaNtunjambili; kalivulwa ngabantu, livulwa yizinkonjane, zan' ezindiza phezulu. Ngivlliele ngingene!" 
  Wathi ukudikibala esekhumbula ukuthi akabange esambuza uLamula ukuthi linjani itshe likaNtunjambili lelo. Waqala ukulibona ngamehlo engqondo kusengathi yitshe eliwubukhazikhazi. Itshe eliyisibuko selanga, elihle kunawo wonke asake wawabona. Mhlawumbe likhulu lingangendlu nje bo. Okanye lingaphezulu kwendlu, yisisekeseke nje sentaba. Kwaba sengathi uyambona uLamula esemi esiqongweni salelitshe, esemude ngokunye. Aphinde ambone futhi uLamula esehlezi enlunjeni yalelitshc uMkabayi yen a ehlezi kwenye intunja ... 
  Wayeka ukucabanga ngetshe, wacabanga ngoLamula uqobo noqobo. Nokho wabathe uyacabanga, umqondo wakhe wadilingana kuhle kwamanzi esiyalu, akaze akwazi akucabangayo. Wazibuza ukuthi ngabe ugcinile yini ukumbona uLamula noma uzophinde ambone futhi? Yikuphi okungcono, ambone noma angomboni? Adidizele uMkabayi. Uma engamboni kungakubi kakhlllu, kungasho ukuthi ubedlala ngaye. Konje umuntu angasuka kude kangaka ezodlala? Qha, uzophinde ambone futhi. Uma-ke esecela impendulo yakhe uzophendula athini? Athi uyamthanda? Athi akamthandi? 
55 




 
Empeleni uyamthanda yini noma akamthandi? Wafisa sengathi kungakhona omelulekayo ngalokhu. Kwaba yikhona ekhumbulayo ukuthi ngisho uTozi, inkosazana kayisekazi uNkwelo wayengakaze ameluleke ngezomagomana. Wayengazi ukuthi isesheli siphendulwa kanjani. Wayazi khona nje ukusiphoxa ukuze sijokole nxa ezwa ukuthi siyamdina. Pho-ke, njengoba uLamula engamdini nje uzomphendula athini? Wazibuza eziphendula uMkabayi wageina esezunywe wubuthongo. 
  Waehiphatheka njalo uLamula waze wayokhuleka kulowomuzi ayengenise kuwona ngayizolo wafike wacela isikhundla. Baphinda bamemukela kahle. Ngenxa yokuthi wayesazizwa izidubuli zendlela en de esuka kwaNgcolosi, washeshe wabeka uhlangothi, walala. Nokho ubuthongo abusheshanga ukufika. Wayenakashelwe yimicabango. Wayeeabanga ngoMkabayi. Isithunzi salentombazane sasilokhu simfakele itwetwe njalo. Wayengakaze ehlulwe yintombi kodwa bkho kakumnikanga isibindi sokuthi noMkabayi uzomehlulao Ngenye-ke lentombazana. Nanxa ingakavuthwa ebuntombini inesithunzi samaqhikiza. Ugazi lwayo lwamukha umfo kaBhengu, wabona ukuthi nxa ingangena emasangweni asesigodlweni 5ikayise, angahalaliselwa kuhle kwesihlabani sibuye empini sin gobile. Nxa engehlulwa nguMkabayi kungangcono angaphinde asikhulumise isidalwa esingumuntu wesifazane. Ukuthi intombi kayimnikanga gama kulokhu akucele kuyo akuzange kumhluphe uLamula. Wayengalindele, vele, ukuba imphendule ngosuku lokugala. Wabonga khona nje ukuba imemukele ngomusa, wathokoziswa yindlela ayibone imkhiyazelela ngayo. 
  Kwase kungena ubusika ngakho amacece aycyinsada. Abanurnzane babekhulisa amantombazane abo, bezihlaba ngazimbili ngazintathu izinkabi, lungekho uvalo lokuthi inyama ingahle yonakale m,1sinya. ISAHLUKO 8 
ISETHEMBISO ESINQALA 
Kwakusekuseni. Izintombi zasezibuya emithonjeni nezimbiza zamanzi emakhanda. lzulu lalembozile kodwa kubonakala ukuthi Iizoshisela emafini. UJama wayesevukile kodwa esalalele umzimha owawusuqala ukuzwela ukuluphala. Phela nokuvuka kwasekuqala ukuba ngumzahalazo. Ingani kwasekuthi nxa evuka kuqhume am3lunga ubunqeklenqekle, lapha emadolweni kube sengathi kukhona unyazi olunyazimayo, iqolo kube sengathi Iinqamukana kabili ngenxa yobuhlungu. Lapho-ke uzombona esebuyise izinhlonze nobuso sebunyukubele. Nokho omdala wayengabonakali ukuthi usekhulile lokhu phela wayeyinsele kalindamkhonto. 
Wazamula kakhulu uJama wazelula esikhumbeni ayehlezi kuso. 
Kuwo lowomnyama kwangena uMmama ethwele izandla ekhanda ekhihla isililo. Ngendlela ayekhala ngayo ngisho uMkabayi wethuka, 
63 




 
wathathela ngejubane kwaba ubugidigidi izintombi ezimbili ziyongena zelakanyana elawini lenkosi. NoJama imbala wathi ukuqikileka: "Yini kangaka, bantabami? Wangena ngesililo, Mmama, kwenzenjani? Udliwa yini? Ngiphuthume bo, Mkabayi, konakeleoi?" 
  "Baba!" kuphendula uMkabayi eheEuzelela phezulu, "Nami angazi, ngibona yen a uMmama lana osedinda isiliJo. Khuluma, Mmama, kodwa kwenzenjani? Udliwa yini, Mmama?" 
  Kube sengathi bayambanga uMmama ngalemibuzo. Akhale ehluleke ukuzibamba. "Maye! Maye ... ! Maye We ... ! Pho, ngomama? Ngiyazisa ngomama!" Kuxake nje ukuthi ngabe unina okade aha mathambo amhlophe ungena ngani kulendaba.

  "Hhi ... ! Hhi ... !Hhi ... ! Umame wakwaDlangaye lona. Umame wakwaDlangaye uthi. .. uthi ... njalo yena nxa engibona uthi ... e .. uthi kimi nansi lenta eyabulala unina."

"Uthini unyoko wakwaDlangaye? Mamoshane! Uthi ngikuzwa kahle kodwa?"

  UMkabayi naye wayengakulindele neze okunje. Kuyena, ukushaqeka kwahlangana nokuthukuthela, wazizwa esegedezela, esengqangqa. uMkabi kube kuhle kudele. Nokho ifu elasibekela ngesikhathi sokuzalwa kukaPhalo Iiphinde Iisibekele futhi, abhubhe umfana esewusana olubomvana. Kubonakale ukuthi isiqalekiso asivumi ukugudluka phezu komuzi wakwaNobamba. 
  Kungaso lesisikhathi okwabuya ngaso isithunywa saseLangeni sesizobika ukuthi ishaka lelo IikaMudli seliphenduke umntwana, uNandi uzibule ngomfana. Pho kwakungabe kusathiwa ngubani igama lomntwana kungasashiwongo ukuthi nguShaka? Inkukhu inqunywe umlomo kwabakwaZulu. Nokho igugu lokuzala Iimeqe uMthaniya. Aye ngasese kuMudli aeele ukuba amenzele ithuba lokubona umzukulu wakhe ngasese. Nebala alenze ithuba uMudli. Alethwe ngesinyelela uShaka kwaNobamba, aHke angeniswe elawini IikaMthaniya. Ngokwesaba ihlazo, kuvinjwe abantu kuthiwe bangangeni elawini likaMthaniya ngoba uyagula, usadla amakhambi enyanga. Pho ngoba abantu abacushwa, basheshe bethwase ukuthi loMthaniya okuthiwa uyagula kukhona umuntu axoxa naye ade emdlalisa. Kuthe kusuka kwase kuduma ukuthi uMthaniya ufuye impaka. ISAHLUKO 14 
UMFULA WEGAZI 
UOingane noMhlangana babemesaba uShaka esaphila kodwa uthe angafa bamesaba kakhulu; bamesaba ukwedlula esaphila. Bathi lapho bembona eselele ethe ja kwaNyakamubi, bampampa beyozithukusa elawini likaMkabayi. Bangena bengasakhulekanga phela nezulu alibanike thuba. Abahlome izimbumbulu zamehlo uMkabayi abuze ukuthi umsebenzi sebewuphethile yini, bavume. Athule uMkabayi, abheke phansi. 
  Kumnyama lapha elawini likaMkabayi. Ubhaqa babe besalokhele lucishwe wumoya 10na owishizayo. Liyaduma izulu. Liduma kungqangqazele izinsika zelawu. Kuthi uma linyampuza umbani ubone ingebhe ilotshwe amabunzini oOingane noMhlangana. Sebejuluke bamanzi te kanti izandla zabo zisaconsa igazi. Yigazi likaShaka leli.

  Ingebhe ibenze babe nezinhliziyo ezincane ababulali. Bayinhlalunhlalu manje abasavumelani. ISAHLUKO 15 
EMGUNGUNDLOVU 
Emva kokubeka kwakhe uDingane esihlalweni, uMkabayi wezwa umzimba wakhe ungenwa ukukhathala okungejwayelekile. Kwakhathala amalunga onke omzimba kwangathi kukhona obewaqoba, kwaze kwakhathala ngisho inhliziyo imbala, kwasengathi kayisafuni ukushaya ngaphakathi kwesifuba sakhe. Wayeze abeke isandla esifubeni, ayizwe ishaya kancane ithu du ... du ... du ... Ngisho inxulurna lakwaDukuza imbala walizwa linesithunzi esinye okungathi siyamemboza, siyamsibekela. Yabe iyinkulu impi ayeyilwile selokhu angena ngamasango kulomuzi omkhulu womntanomfowabo. Manje waycsekhathele. Wayesekhumbule kude enhla nezwe. Wayesekhumbule kwaNobamba. 
  Nokho inhliziyo yakhe yayenelisiwe. Wayazi ukuthi impi uyilwile wayinqoba. Kwase kumfanele ukuba aphindele ekhaya kwaNo- 
167 




 
 
bamba ayophumula ukuze ahlumeleleke.Wamangala lapho ecabanga ngempilo yakhe. Yayithanda ukuba ilokhu ibe ngumqansa njalo. Okwakumvamile kwakungubunzima. Injabulo kwakuba ngeyesikhashana nje ibuye yedlule njengefu, Wabonga nokho ukuthi amathongo akwaMalandela amnike amahlombe abanzi okuthwala yonke imithwalo yesizwe sikayisemkhulu, uNdaba. 
  Nembala wathatha ulwendo olude esephindela emuva, UOingane naye wayengazimisele ukubusela kwaDukuza. Ziningi ezase zcnzeke kulomuzi ezazihlala ziyithunzi njala emcabangweni wakhe. Wabona ukuthi nxa engabusela kulendawo uyohlala engaphansi kwethunzi likaShaka njalo, Nokho wayengafuni ukubuyela emzini kayise eSiklebheni. Naye njengoShaka, wayefuna ukwakha elakhe inxuluma. Kodwa okwakumbalekisa eSiklebheni yen a kwakwehlukile. Wayebaleka ngoba iSiklebhe siseduze kakhulu nakwaNobamba lapho kubusa khona uMkabayi. Wayeneqiniso lokuthi ukuze abuse kubuseke, ashaye umthetho wenziwe, kumele aqhelelane noyisekazi, Wayemesaba uMkabayi. Wayesaba ukuthi nxa eseduze kwakhe kuyogcina elakhe njalo, Wayesekubone kahle lokho bekwaOukuza. 
  Wamakha-ke uqedisigodi wenxulumakazi lakhe wamqamba ngokuthi kuseMgungundlovu. Abaningi labethusa leligama. Phela uDingane wayefuna ukukhumbuza isizwe sonke ngisho izizukulwane eziyolandela ngesigungu esahlangana kwaDukuza ngozungu 10kugiba indlovu enkulu, uShaka, 
Wakha lesisigodlo nje usesovalweni uDingane. Wesaba isizwe. 
Akanaqiniso lokuthi sizomemukela njengenkosi yaso, We saba abantu ababekhonze uShaka. Abone ukuthi yinye kuphela into ezomsiza. Kumele abachazele ukuthi uShaka umbulalele ukukhulula bona. Ngemuva kwalokhu izintombi nezinsizwa zizothola i1ungelo lokuganana kuphele lesiyasihluku sikaShaka sokuyeka izintombi zigugele ezinsisheni, nezinsizwa zize zijutshwe sezingamaxhegu. Abethembise futhi ukuthi abazukuphenduka ukudla kwamanqe kanti futhi ngeke abhuqabhuqe izwe ngezimpi. 
  Lezizethernbiso zibanike ithemba abaningi, Ngisho uMaliwane, inkosi yamaNgwane athi nxa ezizwa abe nesifiso sokuphindcla engabadini yawoyisemkhulu. Phela wayehlupheka Ie ezintabeni zaseCwa, elwa nezizwe zabeSuthu, izinto zingamhambeli kahle. Nebala abuye. Akhonze kuOingane. UOingane amnike indawo khona eduze naseMgungundlovu. Akhe uMatiwane nabantu bakhe, azinze. Kuthe emva kwezinyangana akhile uMatiwane kwase kufika umbiko uvela kuDingane uthi kunabantu abathumbe izinkomo zakhe manje

ucela amaNgwane azomelekelela kubuyiswe lezonkomo, Nebala kurnthokozise uMatiwane ukuthola lelithllba lokllkhombisa llkllbonga kwakhe naye ngokuvunyelwa nguDingane ukuba abuyele ekhaya. Pho, bandla, nabantu bakhe abasengakanani lokhu phe!a wabhuqwa yizimpi zikaManlatisi, umholi wabaTlokwa, Athathe won a lawomakhulwana ambalwa asele anikele kuDingane. Ajabule impela uOingane ebona ukuthi uMatiwane ungumhlobo owethembekile. Amemukele ngomkhulu umusa athi makangene esibayeni eMgungundlovu. Angene bala amaNgwane. Kuthi kusekuhle kunja10, afike namabutho kaDingane azobuyisa izinkomo lezo eziphangiwe. Kuwo 10womnyama ahuze uDingane ukuthi baphi abantu bakaMatiwane. Azikhalele uMatiwane abike ukuthi akasenabantu, ukuphela kwalemithonseJana afike nayo - esho ekhomba amabutho asesibayeni. Aphendukele emabuthweni akhe uDingane athi: 
"Phezu kwabo!" Pho lokhu amabutho abesetshelwe ngaphambili ukuthi umsebenzi okumele awenze yimuphi,ayesebathelekele abantu bakaMaliwane bengalindele. Ashaya ibhuqe, kwangasinda nowokubika. UMatiwane yena kwathiwa angafi ngomkhonto kodwa ephu1we izongo lentamo bese eyolahlwa esiweni kanye nczidumbu zabantu bakhc.Kusukela ngalelolanga, lesosiwa sabizwa ngokuthi isiwa sikaMatiwane. Akone lulho belu uDube, isono ukuthi nje uyisihlobo sikaShaka. Nxa umuntu enganile pho uDingane wayezomhlasela ngambandela muni? nothungo; ufuna kuze ngisho izingane nezalukazi. Nempela ahloniphe uDube, enze njengokuyala kukaDingane. Bathe nje lapho bezethula izintingo ayeseqhamukile amabutho kaDingane. Yasho labalinye induna yabo yathi: "Babambeni!" Ayesephezu kwabo njalo amabutho, egwaza ibhece, abantu bengahlomile. 
  Kuthe ukuba ash aye kole esizweni samaQadi uDingane, wayesebheka ukuthi yibaphi abazolandela. Kwakungabuye kube yibaphi kungebona abakwaCele, ezinye futhi izihlobo zikaShaka. Ubesaba nje abakwaCele, wenqene inkosi yabo uMkhonto, eyayibusa ngobuhlakani obukhulu kanti futhi iyiqhawe. Njengoba nabo abakwaCele kabone .Iutho nje, uDingane abone ukuthi okungcono yikho ukuba abameme ngobungani. Nebala athumele izwi lokuthi ucela abakwaCele bamelekelele bazomakhisa umuzi wend una yakhe, uSotobe, lokhu usezwile ukuthi bayizinyanga zokwakha. Ahloniphe uMkhonto lokhu phela wazi ukuthi kaxabene nendlu kaSenzangakhona. Kusuke isizwe sonke kusale amakhosikazi nezingane kuphela. Nempela Iwakhiwe uthango lomuzi kaSotobe lube luhle lube njeya. Kuthe nxa sebevalelisa abakwaCele wenqaba uSotobe wathi bangehambe engakafiki uDingane. Nebala bahlale babuse ngotshwala, kwenziwe namajadu kube kuhle kudele. Langa limbe, kufike isigijimi nombiko wokuthi ibhubesi selidle inkomo yenkosi. USotobe athi abakwaCele abamelekelele kuyobulawa isilwane leso. Nebala bavume. Banele bangafika endle, abajikele uSotobe, bamuzwe esethi: "Bulalani ibhubesi!" Babe besabheke bangaboni bhubesi, kuphela babone amabutho kaDingane esekhuza isaga ethathela eza kubo. Pho bengengakanani akukho ababengakwenza. Yarisiphezu kwabo impi, kwaphinda esamaQadi.

  Naye uMkabayi uyazizwa lezi esezenziwa nguDingane, indodana yomfowabo ebekwe nguye esihlalweni. Ukuba izindlebe ziyagcwala wukuzwa ngabe ezikaMkabayi zagcwala. Wakhumbula mhla ebingelelwa nguDingane engena ngakho kodwa esigodlweni embalisela ngokuthi uShaka usephenduke inkentshane. Dingane osebusa eMgungundlovu, ezwe edideka uMkabayi. Ngabe wuye lowo noma ngomunye lona? Axakeke impela uMkabayi. Angaze aqonda noma sekwenza ukuthuntubezeka kwengqondo ngenxa yokukhula noma yisimo esididayo nje kunoma yimuphi umuntu omdala nomncane.

Ezwe ukuthi isize yaphindelela kabili phesheya kweGwa ihlasele uMzilikazi kaMashobana. lbe isahlasele ifike ibhuqwe yindlala, ingenwe yimbo engaziwa ngenxa yokubulawa ngamakhaza. Kuzwakale ukuthi uNcaphayi ubalekele kwelamaLawu phansi kwezintaba zoKhahlamba. Impi imlandele khona lapho ifike ibhuqwe yiqhwa nombayiyane. Kufe izinkulungwane zamabutho. Othulasizwe bombuso bafela ezizweni bebhuqwa yimbo nemikhuhlane benqamula amazwe angaziwa ... "

  Udidwa yisimo sezinto ngapha uMkabayi; kanti ngapha udidwa yisililo sabantu bakayise. Bayakhala abantu. Bazikhalela bona. Bakhalela umbuso kaNdaba. Bakhalela ikusasa likaZulu kuloDingane oseMgungundlovu. Sekuyachwaza nje ezindlebeni zikaMkabayi. Kokunye kuba sengathi kuchwaza isihlonono, kokunye kube sengathi kuduma amabhungezi.
